Easy on CPU and memory.\r\nIMPORTANT: uBlock Origin is completely unrelated to the site \"ublock.org\".\r\n\r\n***\r\n\r\nAn efficient blocker: easy on memory and CPU footprint, and yet can load and enforce thousands more filters than other popular blockers out there.\r\n\r\nUsage: The big power button in the popup is to permanently disable/enable uBlock Origin for the current web site. It applies to the current web site only, it is not a global power button.\r\n\r\n***\r\n\r\nFlexible, it's more than an \"ad blocker\": it can also read and create filters from hosts files.\r\n\r\nOut of the box, these lists of filters are loaded and enforced:\r\n\r\n- EasyList\r\n- Peter Lowe‚Äôs Ad server list\r\n- EasyPrivacy\r\n- Malware domains\r\n\r\nMore lists are available for you to select if you wish:\r\n\r\n- Fanboy‚Äôs Enhanced Tracking List\r\n- Dan Pollock‚Äôs hosts file\r\n- hpHosts‚Äôs Ad and tracking servers\r\n- MVPS HOSTS\r\n- Spam404\r\n- And many others\r\n\r\nOf course, the more filters enabled, the higher the memory footprint. Yet, even after adding Fanboy's two extra lists, hpHosts‚Äôs Ad and tracking servers, uBlock Origin still has a lower memory footprint than other very popular blockers out there.\r\n\r\nAlso, be aware that selecting some of these extra lists may lead to higher likelihood of web site breakage -- especially those lists which are normally used as hosts file.\r\n\r\n***\r\n\r\nFree.\r\nOpen source with
